# 研究取引 贈与 分野振り分け

	id = ngm_tech_trade.9
	title = ngm_tech_trade.9.name
	desc = ngm_tech_trade.9.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_intelligence_report

	is_triggered_only = yes
	# 物理学tier1

# 研究取引 贈与 物理学tier1
country_event = {
	id = ngm_tech_trade.10
	title = ngm_tech_trade.10.name
	desc = ngm_tech_trade.10.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_intelligence_report
	show_sound = event_activating_unknown_technology
	is_triggered_only = yes
	# ゼロG研究施設
	option = {
		name = ngm_tech_trade.10.a
		trigger = {
			has_technology = tech_space_science_1
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_global_flag = ngm_technology_trade_tech_space_science_1_global_flag
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = ngm_technology_trade_1_country_flag
				}
				random_country = {
					limit = {
						is_same_empire = event_target:ngm_technology_trade_1
					}
					country_event = {
						id = ngm_tech_trade.25
					}

# 研究取引 贈与 受け取り側
country_event = {
	id = ngm_tech_trade.25
	title = ngm_tech_trade.25.name
	desc = ngm_tech_trade.25.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_intelligence_report
	show_sound = event_activating_unknown_technology
	is_triggered_only = yes
	# 物理学tier1
		# ゼロG研究施設
		option = {
			name = ngm_tech_trade.25.c
			trigger = {
				has_global_flag = ngm_technology_trade_tech_space_science_1_global_flag
			}
			allow = {
				NOT = {
					has_technology = tech_space_science_1
				}
				resource_stockpile_compare = {
					resource = influence
					value >= 50
				}
			}
			add_resource = {
				influence = -50
			}
			give_technology = {
				tech = tech_space_science_1
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				remove_global_flag = ngm_technology_trade_tech_space_science_1_global_flag
				random_country = {
					limit = {
						is_same_empire = event_target:ngm_technology_trade_0
					}
					country_event = {
						id = ngm_tech_trade.26
					}
				}
				add_trust = {
					who = event_target:ngm_technology_trade_0
					amount = 50
				}
			}
		}
		# 量子論
		option = {

		# 管理AI
		option = {
			name = ngm_tech_trade.25.c
			trigger = {
				has_global_flag = ngm_technology_trade_tech_administrative_ai_global_flag
			}
			allow = {
				NOT = {
					has_technology = tech_administrative_ai
				}
				resource_stockpile_compare = {
					resource = influence
					value >= 50
				}
			}
			add_resource = {
				influence = -50
			}
			give_technology = {
				tech = tech_administrative_ai
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				remove_global_flag = ngm_technology_trade_tech_administrative_ai_global_flag
				random_country = {
					limit = {
						is_same_empire = event_target:ngm_technology_trade_0
					}
					country_event = {
						id = ngm_tech_trade.26
					}
				}
				add_trust = {
					who = event_target:ngm_technology_trade_0
					amount = 50
				}
			}
		}

			name = ngm_tech_trade.25.c
			trigger = {
				has_global_flag = ngm_technology_trade_tech_basic_science_lab_3_global_flag
			}
			allow = {
				NOT = {
					has_technology = tech_basic_science_lab_3
				}
				resource_stockpile_compare = {
					resource = influence
					value >= 50
				}
			}
			add_resource = {
				influence = -50
			}
			give_technology = {
				tech = tech_basic_science_lab_3
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				remove_global_flag = ngm_technology_trade_tech_basic_science_lab_3_global_flag
				random_country = {
					limit = {
						is_same_empire = event_target:ngm_technology_trade_0
					}
					country_event = {
						id = ngm_tech_trade.26
					}
				}
				add_trust = {
					who = event_target:ngm_technology_trade_0
					amount = 50
				}
			}
		}
